### System — 2026-07-01T22:37:33.162790

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task**: Execute a full operational health check of the OWL swarm stack using `blofin_get_stack_health` and `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report`. Return strict JSON with fields: `status`, `issues`, `repair_actions`, `confidence`, `narrative`.

**Current Stack Health (2026‑07‑02 02:28 UTC)**  
- Timestamp: 1782959461.5497634  
- Web‑socket cache age: 14 s (fresh)  
- Cycle: 0 (no completed trading cycle)  
- Account equity: $2.66, Available margin: $0.94 (≈35 % of equity)  
- Last error: none  
- Universe: 511 symbols scanned, cache age 42 s, 478 pre‑rank candidates ready  
- Top pick: **TAC‑USDT** (short) – price change ‑33.9 % (journal 0W/0L)  
- Open positions: 1 short **VELVET‑USDT** (size –1, avg 1.5412, mark 1.49744, unrealized +$0.44)  
- Blocked symbols: new sells blocked for **VELVET‑USDT** (the only open position)  
- Positions missing TP/SL: **VELVET‑USDT**  
- Rules enforced: no new buys on blocked‑buy list; no new sells on blocked‑sell list; skip trade if only candidate is blocked; every open position must have TP/SL (`blofin_place_tpsl` / `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl`).  
- API issue: HTTP 429 rate‑limit on `/api/v1/account/balance`; fallback to disk snapshot in use.  

**Recent Self‑Heal**: Swarm applied “TPSL Guard” to auto‑repair positions lacking TP/SL.

**Open Issues Identified**  
1. **Low available margin** ($0.94) limits new trade sizing.  
2. **VELVET‑USDT short lacks TP/SL**, violating safety rule.  
3. **Rate‑limit (429) on balance endpoint** – could affect real‑time equity data.  
4. **Blocked‑sell list contains the only open position**, preventing additional short adds this cycle.  

**Recommended Immediate Repair Actions**  
- Call `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl` (or `blofin_place_tpsl`) for `VELVET‑USDT` to attach default TP/SL.  
- Implement a 2‑minute back‑off on further balance/position API calls; rely on cached equity snapshot until rate limit clears.  
- After diligence completes, re‑rank candidates (`blofin_rank_opportunities`) and, if `TAC‑USDT` remains viable and margin permits, execute the short via `blofin_execute_minimum_trade`.  
- Continuously monitor available margin; size any new position ≤ available × leverage (`_fit_size_to_available`).  

**Next Step**: Invoke `blofin_get_stack_health` and `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report`, combine their outputs, and produce the required JSON summary reflecting the above status, issues, and repair actions, with confidence assessment.

**Swarm Learning Report (as of 2026‑07‑02 02:40:53 UTC)**  

| Category | What happened | Current state / outcome |
|----------|---------------|--------------------------|
| **Total audit events** | 1 227 events processed | – |
| **Last learned issue** | **Missing TP/SL protection** on the open position **VELVET‑USDT**. | The self‑heal playbook automatically ran `audit_open_positions_tpsl()` and attempted to place the missing TP/SL orders. |
| **Self‑fix result** | **TPSL Guard** repaired the missing protection (recorded as a *self_fix*). | Proof shows the position is still **“missing”** after the fix because the API call to place/verify TP/SL hit **HTTP 429 (rate‑limit)**. The guard marks the fix as *fixed* but the pending‑trust remains *failed*. |
| **Rate‑limit impact** | All TP/SL verification calls are being throttled (`Error 1015`). | The playbook added a guard: **“TP/SL verify rate‑limited – not blocking new entries on other symbols.”** This prevents the rate‑limit from halting new trades, but the missing TP/SL remains unresolved until the limit clears. |
| **Verified auto‑heals** | • `task_completion_gap` – fixed mismatched task‑board status.<br>• `polymorphic_mesh_incomplete` – noted only 3 of 15 expected agents fulfilled (Portfolio‑Manager, Sentiment‑Agent, Quant‑Analyst).<br>• `surface_sync_drift` – dashboard UI missing markers (`mesh_fulfillment`, `clique_rugged`, etc.) and was auto‑updated.<br>• `missing_tpsl` – flagged and recorded as repaired, though actual TP/SL placement still pending due to rate‑limit. | Each of these items shows a **“verified_fix”** entry confirming the playbook’s corrective action. |
| **Mesh fulfillment** | Only **3 / 15** agents reported as fulfilled. | Pending agents include Trading‑Director, Ops‑Monitor, Verifier, Tactics‑Researcher, Profit‑Strategist, Market‑Researcher, Risk‑Manager, Execution, and all Pentest agents. No “weak agents” reported yet. |
| **Surface‑sync drift** | Dashboard UI lost markers that display mesh fulfillment and clique ruggedness. | Playbook auto‑healed by updating `swarm_dashboard.html`, the graph API, and related prompt/playbook files. |
| **Current warnings** | • **HTTP 429** on `/api/v1/trade/orders-tpsl-pending` and `/api/v1/account/positions` for VELVET‑USDT.<br>• Rate‑limit skip flag is set, meaning the guard will **not block new trades** while verification fails. | Until the rate‑limit clears, the TP/SL for VELVET‑USDT remains unprotected. |
| **Last autonomous fix** | TPSL Guard repaired missing protection (recorded at 02:40:53). | Same rate‑limit issue persists; the fix is logged as successful but the underlying API error remains. |
| **Improvement metric** | No measurable improvement logged yet. | The system is still learning how to handle persistent rate‑limits. |

### Key Take‑aways
1. **Missing TP/SL on VELVET‑USDT** is the primary operational issue; the guard attempted a fix but was blocked by Cloudflare rate‑limiting (HTTP 429).  
2. **Rate‑limit handling** is now baked into the guard (skip flag, do‑not‑block‑new‑entries), but the actual protection is still pending.  
3. **Mesh fulfillment** is low (3/15 agents), indicating many agents have not completed their cycle this round.  
4. **Dashboard UI** was out‑of‑sync; the playbook corrected the missing markers.  
5. **No improvement metrics** yet – the swarm needs further cycles to verify that the TP/SL protection is finally applied once the rate‑limit subsides.
